    <h2 class="generated-specs__title">Audi Q6 Sportback e-tron performance</h2>
    <div class="generated-specs__groups">
      <section class="generated-specs__group">
        <h3>Fahrleistung</h3>
        <div class="generated-specs__group-body">
      <div class="spec-row"><span class="spec-row__label">Spitzenleistung</span><strong class="spec-row__value">225 kW (306 hp / 302 bhp)</strong></div>
      <div class="spec-row"><span class="spec-row__label">Spitzenleistung mit Boost</span><strong class="spec-row__value">240 Kw</strong></div>

      <div class="spec-row"><span class="spec-row__label">Höhenverstellbare Kopfstütze</span><strong class="spec-row__value">Serienausstattung</strong></div>
      <div class="spec-row"><span class="spec-row__label">Tiefenverstellbare Kopfstütze</span><strong class="spec-row__value">Nicht verfügbar</strong></div>
